padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2327132" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ChloeG118"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1850006"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="ChloeG118" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/J-Scent/Yawahada-Soft-Skin-56088.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.56088.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Yawahada (Soft Skin)"title="Yawahada (Soft Skin)"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2327132ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2327132" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1850006">ChloeG118</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-25">10/25/24 07:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is a lovely fall fragrance. It's warm, woody, ambery, and the vanilla accord has a welcome, solid presence without being that sweet. I often dislike vanilla, so if you do too, just know that it's not sugary here. It's coming from the tonka, which is vanilla's flatter, less sweet cousin. The primary note for me is that tonka bean and the amber, but the woody notes darken it a bit and the cognac gives it a bit of life without being boozy. Overall, this scent is smooth, mature, cozy, and just a little sexy.<br />
<br />
I honestly feel like this is a unisex fragrance; I have no problem wearing it as a woman. I understand the reviews saying it's nice but nothing innovative, and while I tend to agree, it's executed very well. Whether it's worth the money to you is a different question, but it's undeniably a good fragrance. Worth picking up a decant, in my opinion, and adding this cozy  cool weather scent to your roster. 8.5/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="2327132"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=2327132#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2319863" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Not much to write about because there's nothing impressive about it, just a very safe profile and it did it job very well. An iconic one, the first comes to mind when you think of its profile. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/36833">Enrium</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-18">08/18/24 03:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The Tragedy of Lord George is, like most Penhaligon's scents, a good-quality scent that is classic in style but with limited performance. LG is a fairly simple balsamic amber scent, smooth and pleasant throughout. <br />
<br />
LG has a boozy opening, not overwhelming, but smooth and warm, paving the way to the deeper amber accord that defines this scent. The amber is smooth and sweet with a vanilla nuance. The woody notes follow after a little while, the perfect accompaniment to the balsamic amber. I get the tonka bean note at the drydown phase, adding to the sweet smoothness and lingering until final fade. Sillage and longevity are moderate at a push -  I would expect better performance from a scent of this profile and price point. It is a transeasonal daytime scent.<br />
<br />
A pleasant, discreet masculine-leaning balsamic scent, LG is a decent example of its genre. It is an elegant everyday scent, smooth and well-rounded with no harshness, but certainly overpriced. 3.5/5.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="2253010"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=2253010#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2249533" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2094708">ghostwriter574</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-25">07/25/24 15:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>One of my favorite hypermasculine scents. 1800s men's club feels right to me - boozy, barbershop-y, and masculine. Smells a bit like shaving cream but I love that, and this is the best "shaving cream" fragrance I've tried. <br />
<br />
My only issue is it doesn't last as long as you'd think it would for being a woody, barbershop fragrance. I only get about 4 hours. But what you sacrifice in longevity you gain in scent - I bet if they made it longer lasting it would come across too strong or synthetic. It's a perfect scent for what it is trying to do.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="2229387"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=2229387#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2229133" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It’s masculine and spicy but not at all scratchy or aggressive, which I love! I definitely get woods and spice, and I can understand where people get a brandy/rum smell from. If I were a guy or enjoyed masculine scents more, I think I might buy this! I also think it’s suitable year round, not too cloying for summer imo.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="2105369"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=2105369#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2104506" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2104506" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="WildCalifornia"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2036447"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="WildCalifornia" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2104506ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2104506" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2036447">WildCalifornia</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-26">03/26/24 04:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Very masculine, it's strong but not offensive. I purchased the discovery set and this was one I was expecting to be whatever about . It's very smooth and bold. The woodsy notes are very prominent and are strong from start until the fragrance fades . The tonka , amber and brandy really round it out. The brandy is the weakest of the notes . Once it dries down it does have a bit of a soap bar smell to it. After about an hour it gets slightly powdery as well.  It really is a luxurious and sophisticated scent and does give off a very gentleman vibe . While not over complex you can tell the ingredients in this are very high quality . Not a young man's fragrance but also not something for grandpa . I would call this a classic that was modernized. Performance is above average. It projects for a good 2 to 3 hours  and will stay on the skin pretty strong for about 4 hours. It completely fades away after about 6 hours . The biggest negative is the price . It's so expensive and I feel something similar could be found for at least half the price .<br />
Scent - 8.5<br />
Complexity - 8.0<br />
Quality - 10.0<br />
Performance -7.5<br />
Bottle - 10.0</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="2104506"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=2104506#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2099391" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; He spent most of his life in the basement, enshrouded in cigar smoke and mephitic gin vapors — his musty sacrosanct solitude. He died before he could ignore me like the rest of his family. I sit with him now in his man-den, we watch his mounted heads desiccate and we talk about the porn he buys on 16mm film. I think he's poorer than me but he seems richer, this is his palace after all.<br />
<br />
Years past I would sit and drink and sit and drink and drink like he did. I don't anymore though and I'm less of a man for it.<br />
<br />
Sillage is moderate, longevity is good.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="2018677"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=2018677#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2010067" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1892188">smelling.sniffing.swan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-12-19">12/19/23 10:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Lord George greets us with a healthy splash of gin. I get a thick herbality in the opening, evocative of an early 1900s medicinal botanical ointment, or one of those essential-oil rollers. There's a sharpness in the opening that I find pretty unpleasant.<br />
This fragrance completely shifts in character in the dry-down.<br />
Suddenly some lightly rose-fragranced talcum powder appears, with some soft woods and an airyness that certainly didn't exist in the more suffocating opening. I definitely understand the comparisons that have been drawn to an old-timey barbershop, and shaving cream. Much more pleasant olfactory experience in the dry-down phase.<br />
<br />
VERDICT: Interesting, but definitely not sexy.<br />
This fragrance's harsh opening detracts from it's overall appeal. However, very pleasant in the dry down.<br />
This would suit a much older man. Not grandfather, GREAT grandfather.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="2005291"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=2005291#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2001592" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Something definitely I've smelled before in the past (20 years ago) as I recurrently have with this house so far. Think of an older barbershop/shaving cream and a masculine leaning scent.<br />
<br />
After initial spray. OMG YES! was my reaction. <br />
Any season, any reason. But this shines best in colder weather. Both day or night.<br />
<br />
For me it's an 10/10 as an older person (40 years old)<br />
<br />
Only downside for me is the price. Hoping for a full 100 dollar price slash during the Holidays. Then it would definitely be worth it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1979261"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1979261#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1975520" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1974039" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Llessurx"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1868916"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Llessurx" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1974039ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1974039" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1868916">Llessurx</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-11">11/11/23 07:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Did a blind test on a sample of this. Covered the labels of multiple samples, wore them for a day then removed the label only after I reviewed. <br />
<br />
I actually found this scent quite unusual. I didn’t initially attribute it to a man’s fragrance. It felt 100% unisex to me. Opens up with a note I couldn’t identify, clearly that was Rum although it wasn’t what I expected. Fades off to a lovely warm amber, very comforting while still being sexy. <br />
<br />
Beautiful fragrance and quite powerful. Personally I think this would be too heavy to wear as an every day fragrance or in the office. Two small sprays was more than enough. I did get a headache but I’m not sure if that was directly due to the fragrance or something else. To me it smelt very sexy, the amber note was strong and reminded me somewhat of Catholic Church. On a guess I thought this would be a musky, very niche, incense type fragrance and was quite surprised to see the name. I didn’t imagine it would be so complex. <br />
<br />
Will definitely be buying a bottle. Probably my favourite of the 20 fragrances I blind tested.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1974039"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1974039#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1958626" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1733487">JusttheFactsMan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-10-14">10/14/23 18:46</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>#271 in my "Tour de Fragrance"<br />
<br />
The "tragedy" is all the over-the-top gushing in these reviews. Must be the cool bottle.<br />
<br />
Men: Do yourself a solid and order "WSP Luxury Rustic Shaving Soap" (Black Amber Vanilla) available on Amazon.com, $29.99 for the 4oz jar. A little pricey for shaving cream, but it goes a long way. I like it, and if you like this fragrance, so will you. It's a comforting amber, myrrh, musk and vanilla shaving cream that makes the morning scrape a relaxing pleasure. I can also recommend the Gaelic Tweed, and for you wood lovers the Sandalwood and Mahogany versions as well. I haven't yet tried the Tobacco and Barbershop versions, but they're on my list. <br />
<br />
My point being this fragrance is a scent of no particular distinction. You've smelled all this before. You know you have. Kilian, Tom Ford, Jean Paul Gaultier, Akro, Micallef, Maison Francis Kirkdjian, Maison Martin Margiela, Givenchy, Dior, Chanel, Viktor &amp; Rolf, Versace, Mont Blanc, and every Arab house you can name has done this DNA to death (with or without citrus!). You can't swing a cat without hitting a designer that's done multiple versions of this same kind of scent, of which I have at least a dozen, most of which perform better and at least half of which cost much less. <br />
<br />
But hey, if the deer head bottle and fancy English title makes you feel like you're a-horse on a fox hunt every time you spray this on, I don't judge.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1944320" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="MKnocker"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1583026"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1583026.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="MKnocker" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-Cologne-51692.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.51692.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Aventus Cologne"title="Aventus Cologne"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1944320ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1944320" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1583026">MKnocker</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-10-04">10/04/23 18:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The first hour or so reminds me very much of Creeds Original Santal. Maybe my nose is broken or the sample from the discovery set is from a funky batch. I don’t see OS in the reminds me of section. It starts off woody and spicy like OS. <br />
<br />
This transitions to a more clean/soapy fragrance with just a hint of spice as it reaches the mid. Somewhat barbershop but not quite as barbershop as Santorial. But now it’s just a skin scent. So the beautiful mid is wasted. I have to shove my wrist up to my nose to smell it. Which I keep doing because it’s fantastic. <br />
<br />
It’s a quality perfume. I’d say leans late fall through winter. I would not wear this in the summertime or even on really sunny days. Feels like a cold cloudy or snowy day type of fragrance. <br />
<br />
At over $200 for 75 ml at a discounter it’s tough to justify. If the performance was better I would absolutely be a buyer at that price because it’s a very nice high quality perfume. But if it doesn’t perform then what’s the point? <br />
<br />
Will edit this review after a few more wears if my opinion changes over time. This would be one I would cross my fingers and hope it would macerate a lot.<br />
<br />
Edit: Did left arm/right arm test with this and Original Santal. They’re 75% the same. The brandy changes things a bit for George and it’s a little woodier and less spicy. But it’s pretty damn close. If you like Original Santal or Montblanc Individuel I think you’ll like this. Performance is not good though. And it’s more expensive than Original Santal. Which performs better and is the better fragrance imo.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1944320"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1944320#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1937571" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Would recommend trying it on skin before buying as I almost made an expensive mistake.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1889796"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1889796#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1880113" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1710835">TBonetheFella</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-05-31">05/31/23 12:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I got this while on tour of London awhile back, and I spray it on me every once in awhile to remember that trip and reminisce on the fun memories I made.<br />
<br />
Now that I have been back in the states for awhile, I wanted to take the time to really smell this perfume and judge it not based off the memories I have with it or the company that surrounds it; but the smell in of itself.<br />
<br />
And man, when I compare it to some of the other stuff I have in my collection, I am sorely disappointed.<br />
<br />
Not saying it's not good, it is good! It's just very... boring. Like this would make the perfect office fall/winter scent with how safe and woody it is very classy and warm. Super linear too, the woods just get more and more cedar like as time goes on, but again that's not a bad thing. I just wish that I didn't pay the amount of money that I did at the time. Hindsight will always be 20/20 I guess, but for a general scent it's good, nothing to write home about, but still good. Unlike a lot of people, I get pretty decent performance and silage out of this, and I commonly wear this when dressing formal for an event or a winters night where I want to feel classy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Beige as in non-descript, non playable character, a brown noise woody accord painted with a tepid "boozy" note (snores and zzzzzzzzz's) and a "compliments bro" coumarin fluffernutter.<br />

The opening smells of high-end natural bar soap (soft, toned down lavender, fir, and natural oils) and shaving products. When it starts to settle, the boozy note becomes more prominent. It smells like some kind of cognac or rum that is smoothened out by the addition of tonka bean. Besides this, it has some ambery and woody facets that add depth and character.<br />
Usually (at least according to my experience), most soapy fragrances are cold and fresh. This, however, is both soapy and very warm at the same time. It smells like an expensive, steamy barbershop with wooden interior and barbers wearing flat caps, button-down shirts, and suspenders, who offer you whiskey when you enter their shop. I feel like a king when I wear this fragrance. Too bad it is so expensive.... it gets a 9/10 from me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1835107"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1835107#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1834025" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; overall I gave it a 8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1765371"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1765371#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1760126" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1598503">Maliken</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-02-14">02/14/23 15:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I tried a whole bunch of scents from the Portraits collection and The Tragedy of Lord George is one of the better ones from the male oriented fragrances. It smells classy and mature, I don’t think this scent would fit someone below the age of 20. It’s a wonderful boozy scent backed up by woods and a creamy, warm touch of amber.<br />
<br />
Performance is disappointing and not doing it any favors when weighing it up against the retail price and its competition. In fact, for a similar scent profile I would rather turn to  Penhaligon’s own Halfeti Cedar. It’s less expensive, smells more complex and has much better performance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1760126"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1760126#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1758793" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1587643">Soerdjo</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-02-13">02/13/23 01:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I got a 2021 batch of this perfume. I do smell tobacco on the top note, but mainly incense on the middle note. The base note is woody incense with a hint of amber in it. Not a compliment-generator to the crowd, but unique and appreciated.<br />
<br />
The projection is weak, but I think it is appropriate, as a strong one will be too overwhelming for people around.<br />
<br />
For the performance, it is quite disappointing in hot weather but is amazing in colder temperatures. I was wearing this at 20C and it smells amazing, but when I went to the Southern part of Taiwan (approx 30C) the smell magically (disappointingly) disappeared, without a trace. However, it does reappear when I re-enter the cold (can still smell it on elbow-length 8 hours after). I guess it just does not perform under a hot climate.<br />
<br />
Overall, I love the smell. Overpriced, but often available at discount. It is truly a winter/spring perfume, as it does not perform during hotter times.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1758793"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1758793#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1749373" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/21613">Fleurie20</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-02-01">02/01/23 19:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Not listed but there's a tobacco note, which is especially potent when first spray. Then when settles, it smells like a soft, calm, mature type of scent for an older man w the tobacco still lingering in the background. I find the comment by CodyHowl absolutely accurate (re-posting here for your convenience):<br />
<br />
CodyHowl 10/04/21 09:33<br />
<br />
Classically masculine, vintage shaving cream fragrance. Overly blended to the point that none of the individual notes are particularly distinguishable. Clean and sterile, but not "soapy", if that makes sense. This is a very mature, old school frag. Even at 32, I feel like I'd be dating myself by donning this one. Best suited to a man in his forties or beyond.<br />
<br />
While not listed, there is something a bit pipe tobacco-y here. It stains the fragrance the way pipe smoke marries into the fabric of a winter coat oft smoked in. There's also a talc note I'm picking up, also not listed. Overall, I'm not wowed by this one. I've worn plenty of Penhaligon's offerings in the past and found most of them more enjoyable. Perhaps if this was a bit boozier, or even toeing more toward warm gourmand territory, but in its current state it's just an expensive and forgettable shaving cream.<br />
<br />
I could see this as a very nice and novel gift for an older man in your life, like a classy father-in-law who wants to smell nice without giving it too much thought. But I wouldn't buy this for myself.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1749373"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1749373#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1742183" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I stupidly passed up on an opportunity to buy the full presentation for $200 American at duty-free in Germany. rinlux below me describes the scent well but I'd add that the shaving cream is made with 70-year-old whiskey. The pricing of this reminds me of how luxury brands can command a bloated price IF they offer the best version of the scent profile. Creed can charge a premium price for Aventus because it's still the best of its type, Louis Vuitton is the same for its fragrances. Same with Chanel. I guess in these cases it's up to the consumer how strongly they want the frag or how little the money means to them. The final analysis is this is a great fragrance, the best I've tried in the masculine Fougere style old-world sophistication mold, and I may have been an idiot for not jumping on the duty-free bottle but I'll console myself by remembering the sillage isn't that great.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; The dry down is wonderful; we’re talking lavender &amp; sweet amber coexisting with shaving soap.<br />
<br />
Upon application of 3 sprays, this will project within an arms length for 30-45 minutes before settling closer to the skin, to be appreciated via occasional whiffs and by those sharing your intimate space. Personally, I find that this is the perfect way to enjoy a scent such as this. This is a calming &amp; thoughtful fragrance, not one to boast about it’s presence.<br />
<br />
A year would pass from the time that I had first tried this scent, to the point that I decided to commit to a full bottle. Originally, I had only smelt this on a tester strip, pressed up to my nose. Avoid smelling this straight from the atomiser, apply this to your skin and enjoy it in the air as it should be appreciated. <br />
<br />
Lastly, this leans masculine however I would consider this to be unisex. This is a versatile fragrance that is best enjoyed in cooler weather; day or night, casual or formal. I wear this fragrance on lazy, rainy Sundays as well as to the office beneath a white-collared shirt.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1687199"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1687199#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1683580" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1642474" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="farzadkaya"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1059713"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="farzadkaya" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Floris/Elite-5545.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.5545.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Elite"title="Elite"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1642474ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1642474" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1059713">farzadkaya</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-09-10">09/10/22 18:43</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>این عطر واقعا ارزش حتی کمتر از نصف قیمت که هیچ یک‌سوم قیمتی که امثال  فروشگاه نوبهار روی آن گذاشته اند، یعنی هشت تا نه میلیون تومن ندارد. من در شرایط کنونی که پولمان بی ارزش شده حقیقتا حاضر نیستم حتی سه تومن بابت این عطر بپردازم چرا که هیچ چیز متمایز و چشمگیری ندارد بلکه از هر جهت یک کار متوسط اما دارای کیفیت خوب است. در مقایسه با مثلا بارول مین نیویورک که هردو مشروبی و چوبی اند(گرچه بارول کاملا بوزی مشروبی ناب و تراژدی یک تراژدی واقعی از پرداخت متوسط چوبی با پیش زمینه مشروبی است) تراژدی نه از حیث کیفیت و نه پرفورمنس و نه حتی پرداخت هنری و ریزه کاریهای شگفتی که در بارول ما را به وجد می آورد، قابل مقایسه با بارول مین نیویورک نیست، و البته قابل مقایسه با بیشمار کارهای نیش وودی مشروبی نیست.<br />
اما درباب خود کار باید بگم اولین اسپری یک ارائه آشنا و تقریبا خوبی از چوب را به ما می دهد که من تردید ندارم نت هایی از نوع اسپیسی شاید هم انواع چوب ها بویژه سدار در آن هست. این مهمترین نت غالب که در درای داون معتدل میشه و همراه برندی که تند نیست و حتی خیلی هم برندی نیست بلکه باید گفت برندی که احتمالا خواسته ادای شامپاین دربیاره(منظورم این که حس مشروبی تند یا حتی سنگین درش نیست و بعد چندساعت توی درای داون به سختی میشه مرزش از دانه تونکا و کهربا تشخیص داد و البته مهمترین حسن این عطر که اونو برازنده عنوان تراژدی میکنه همین هارمونی این سه نت است که اگر این هارمونی در درای داون نبود حقیقتا ارزش کار به صفر می رسید اما باوجود این هارمونی که درعین حال نمیتونی توش تمایزی بین نت ها برقرار کنی و این عجیب جالب، عطر تراژدی لرد جیمز بدل به اثر فاخری میشه که هرچی ازش میگذره درواقع به گونه ای عجیب همراه با افول پرفورمنس و پخش بوی آن شاهد اعتلای هنری و گرفتن یک دستمریزاد هنری هستیم)! خلاصه در ابتدا تا نیم‌ساعت فضای وودی بوزی مشروبی نیمه سنگینی داریم که بنظر من اصلا چنگی به دل نمیزنه چرا که مثلا اگه قرار باشه با یکی از کارهای له آرتی آن پرفیوم که من چندسال پیش از پرفیوم شاپینگ خریدم و فوربلیس 60بود اسمش اگه اشتباه نکنم و مجسمه کوچک زنبور روش بود، نت چوبی این عطر در برابر اون واقعا پشه در برابر عقاب چرا که اون شاهکاری ناب بود با هزار عشوه گری و این حتی درحد کارهای متوسط گرلن و هرمس(لاین های بازاریشون منظورم وگرنه این دو خانه عطر هزاران بار غنی تر و برتر از خانه عطرهای ترکی ساز انگلیسی پنهالیگون).<br />
زیاد نوشتم اما خلاصه بگم واقعا اگر تست نکردید هیچ چیز از دست ندادید و اگر خریدید قطعا هنگفت ضرر کردید چرا که در هر زمان و هرجایی با اون هزینه میتونستید چندکاره عالی بمراتب بهتر از این بگیرید.<br />
پخش متوسط و ماندگاری خیلی خوب. کیفیت در مقایسه با هزینه واقعا ضعیف، خاص بودن که اصلا هیچ چیز خاصی نداره حتی برای منی که سر کارم شب و روز با شکسپیر و ادبیات و خاصه تعریف آلبر کامو از تراژدی(رگه ای از تلاش موریلاس برای ارائه ای کامجویی از این داستان تاریخی بریتانیایی را میشه در درای داون دید که اونم احتمالا نتیجه پیش داوری ذهن آشنا با مسئله مذکور است)،<br />
درکل اگر برخلاف میلم کار مبتذل نمره دادن را انتخاب کنم قطعا نمره مردود به این عطر میدم. اما گمان نکنید که این عطر دیگه لزوما درحد دانهیل و بولگاری و ورساج و.. است! (حداقل به باور من از کل عطرهای خانه هیستوری پارفیوم بهتر، به استثنای مارکی دو ساد!)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1642474"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1642474#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1631221" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This one is a barbershop in a bottle.  Powdery soapy musky. A little wood. Tonka Tonka coumarin. <br />

I think the “tragedy” is that this, and nearly every single Penhaligon’s scent I’ve tried in the past 15 years, has such disappointing longevity.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1555563" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Ysu"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1469863"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1469863.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Ysu" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1555563ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1555563" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1469863">Ysu</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-05-02">05/02/22 14:11</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Look. I love Penhaligon's as a company. As an avid researcher of anything niche and interesting, I fell in love with their history, aesthetic, and products... on the surface. <br />
<br />
I adore the Portraits line and the little stories they spun for it. <br />
<br />
That being said, Penhaligon's has always fallen a little flat for me. Most of their products smell fine, but definitely not worthy of their /giant/ price tags. The Tragedy of Lord George is a clean, masculine smell reminiscent of an aged sitting room, a glass of whiskey and a cold cigar resting on a tray. What really gets me about Lord George is that it reminds me of Diptyque's Orpheon with absolutely no body. Orpheon develops and is bigger than life, while Lord George dissipates, leaving you with as much sillage as an aftershave.<br />
<br />
Lord George is a dapper grey fox with no substance. The only merits to his name are his fortune and reputation, of which he does not live up to. <br />
<br />
Is it a neat scent? Sure. Is it worth $300? Absolutely not.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1555563"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1555563#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1529671" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1526907" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="purplenoon"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1311284"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1311284.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="purplenoon" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Givenchy/Gentleman-Eau-de-Parfum-48476.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.48476.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Gentleman Eau de Parfum"title="Gentleman Eau de Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1526907ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1526907" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1311284">purplenoon</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-03-20">03/20/22 07:35</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I applied some of The Tragedy of Lord George from a sample before meeting friends for drinks at a cocktail bar, and it made me feel like a million dollars. Walking down the street I would catch whiffs of this that would make my heart skip, and rolling into the bar and taking off my scarf was one of the highlights of my week.<br />
<br />
This has a gorgeously sweet opening, warm and boozy but with a refreshing woodsy undertone and a faint pepper on top. As the pepper subsides, the amber comes out in full force, enveloping the wearer in a golden aura with a soapy undertone, a cross between Prada’s Amber Pour Homme and YSL’S Parfum Intense (incidentally, two of my favourite scents ever). The drydown is a spicy amber. All of this is masterfully blended; a stunning, stunning scent.<br />
<br />
While the scent itself is impeccable, the longevity is indeed a problem, as many have already noted. The fact that this barely lasts through a dinner party (at the end of which it is entirely a skin scent) is indeed the true Tragedy of Lord George. That said, I can’t bring myself to give it any less than a “love” in the ratings for this reason as the scent is just that good. It evokes old school sophistication and elegance while being entirely modern. Perfect for fall and winter, to enjoy with a nice scotch and in good company.<br />
<br />
EDIT: After another wear, I am indeed knocking Lord George down a peg to a "like" and not a "love" - a lesson learned for me not to be so enamoured by a fragrance on the first wear to the point where I entirely overlook its performance. While I do believe there is an ephemerality to fragrance that makes performance a matter of relative conditioning, I can't help but lament the fact that, on me, this turns into a skin scent in well under two hours. Maybe it's me and not Lord George; but in any case, it's gonna be a "like" for this sophisticated under-performer from me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1526907"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1526907#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1521677" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; ⚫️⚫️⚪️⚪️⚪️<br />
<br />
A very nice cashmeran and amber tinged fougere. Without all the prestige of Penhaligons’ branding and pricing, this smells like a JOOP! Homme flanker. Which is perfectly fine at £20-30 but when you’re being charged £210 / 75ml sealed with a gaudy bottle, you are being taken for a ride my friend. <br />
<br />
Anybody worth their salt in this hobby will have an understanding as to how insanely out of whack the quality to cost ratio is. I strongly urge anybody who likes this fragrance to seek it elsewhere.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1504293"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1504293#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1501768" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1286681">arvisk</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-02-10">02/10/22 12:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Hmm, all I get is just soap in a dry down. A heavy-duty laundry soap with slight aromatic undertones.<br />
The first minutes gave some woody and spicy notes but that's all. Maybe, this one needs more chances?</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1501768"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1501768#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1497924" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1485040" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="humphryclinker"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1411704"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1411704.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="humphryclinker" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1485040ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1485040" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1411704">humphryclinker</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-01-17">01/17/22 09:10</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The Tragedy of Lord George is a pleasant, well-rounded amber scent. It is highly adaptable to the office or restaurant, to the park or to the club. I appreciate the versatility of this fragrance where the tonka and vetiver notes ground the amber, keeping it from becoming cloyingly sweet or too thin. Indeed, I think that's why other reviewers are quick to affirm that this is a "masculine" amber scent – there is nothing saccharine or floral here. Overall, it would be a highly rated scent for me if it weren't for the sillage and longevity. With four sprays, others can only smell it in an actual embrace, and I can barely smell it after two hours. I don't mind this if a perfume stays under $200 (or is highly inventive), but as of this review, a 75ml bottle of this EDP is $295. At that price, it needs to do better with performance before I would buy a full bottle. Nevertheless, if you have been looking for an amber fragrance that is more earthy, more solid, then you will love this one.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1485040"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1485040#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1484054" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1310820">sisina96rv</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-12-31">12/31/21 04:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I am testing it for few days as a woman...<br />
I like it.<br />
<br />
Anyone smelling vetiver?<br />
<br />
For me, it is a nicely done vetiver. At first, I smelled a lot of brandy and I guessed patchouli along with smoked woods. If you know M. Margiela Autumn Vibes, you can smell similar notes. Wet earth, decaying fallen leaves, powderiness. And here you add the brandy and shaving foam to the concoction. <br />
After 20-30 minutes it gets sweeter and more rounded, the patchouli dissappears and stays the vetiver dipped in a vanilla - rum creamy  pudding. And this lasts for a few hours. On my skin 8-10 hours, only the projection fades over time, it stays close to you. That is really good if you want to appear as a refined gentleman. And that's the point. This is not a scent for a macho from Despacito 😁, this is more Christian Grey scent (50 shades of grey) 👨💼. And I mean a confident, successful, ambitious man, he might be younger, but he is definitely determined and knows what he wants. And acts and dresses accordingly. This is not a sexi scent, I feel that a man wearing this scent is someone whom I can rely on. He is strong and caring. <br />
Probably that's why people compare the perfume to a "grandpa" scent. My both grandpas wore perfumes and yes, there is something vintage-y and classy about this scent. But I find it very appropriate and noble for a man who is a true provider, a trustworthy support for a woman.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1473762"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1473762#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1465936" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It smells like a fancy, woody, spicy, soap bar, that is a tad on milder side, but it does not give me a headache when applied to my neck, so It gets points for that! Overall for me, a 10ml decant at decent price is definitely worth having and would last me a good while! Ive received more compliments with this fragrance than any other in my collection. I believe this may be because it resonates with me very well. I couldn’t be happier with this fragrance. <br />
<br />
10/10 🦌👑</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1428887"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1428887#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1422244" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/417752">CodyHowl</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-10-04">10/04/21 09:33</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Classically masculine, vintage shaving cream fragrance. Overly blended to the point that none of the individual notes are particularly distinguishable. Clean and sterile, but not "soapy", if that makes sense. This is a very mature, old school frag. Even at 32, I feel like I'd be dating myself by donning this one. Best suited to a man in his forties or beyond.<br />
<br />
While not listed, there is something a bit pipe tobacco-y here. It stains the fragrance the way pipe smoke marries into the fabric of a winter coat oft smoked in. There's also a talc note I'm picking up, also not listed. Overall, I'm not wowed by this one. I've worn plenty of Penhaligon's offerings in the past and found most of them more enjoyable. Perhaps if this was a bit boozier, or even toeing more toward warm gourmand territory, but in its current state it's just an expensive and forgettable shaving cream.<br />
<br />
I could see this as a very nice and novel gift for an older man in your life, like a classy father-in-law who wants to smell nice without giving it too much thought. But I wouldn't buy this for myself.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1422036"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1422036#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1421440" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It's a great addition to my barbershop Fougere collection, and especially the bottle, which looks fantastic next to my MDCI Invasion Barbare bottle with the Ceasar bust cap!<br />
I was trying to think what other fragrance this smells most like, because it triggered my scent memory. Funny, it took a little while but it suddenly dawned on me: Sartorial by Penhaligon. Most of the other supposed "comparisons" on the "this perfume reminds me of..." list on this page are ridiculous. Perhaps it's because the notes and accords list on this page are not accurate. There is a "shaving foam" accord (or notes) not listed here that is central to the scent profile. If that was represented here then I think more people would vote more fougeres, especially of the barbershop variety, onto the list.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1361577">Thanasis_87k</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-09-13">09/13/21 08:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>There is a booziness on the first sprays which is more intense during the first 15-30 minutes, then it becomes much more subtle and is incorporated into the sweet soapy core. The soapiness that other commenters describe is rather rich, I would also add. Sprayed on my arm for the first time, I got plenty of woodsy note(s) especially after the first hour, however spraying it on my neck, provided the aforementioned impression of soapy scent. Strange.<br />
It is long lasting (8rs plus) and its projection seems intimate-moderate. The spray nozzle is great, allowing perfume to spread in large parts of the body.<br />
A glorified barber-shop scent is associated mostly with day time. However this is a serious perfume, which could be supported only by smart dress or a 3 piece suit. Could be an office scent. The notes are Male leaning. Lovely, yet overpriced.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1409621"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1409621#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1402351" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/27512">fragaholic79</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-09-01">09/01/21 00:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The Tragedy of Lord George was the first Penhaligons scent I ever encountered, and I have been in love with it ever since. I’m sure there are others like me who like to wear men’s perfumes. Fragrances should not define genders. <br />
Wearing it takes me to a cold winters day in the woods. A stately manor stands not too far away. Lord George is sitting by the fire, entertaining some gentlemen friends in his oak panelled library. Freshly shaved, the aroma of his expensive shaving soap is mingling with the brandy in his hand. He’s trying to keep up appearances amidst his enduring tragedy. The sweet tonka bean is the ray of light that evokes some hope within him. Alas,this too shall pass.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1402351"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1402351#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1381156" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1263755">The Wolf</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-07-25">07/25/21 01:19</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The main accords and comparison fragrances are totally wrong. <br />
Vanilla? Nope<br />
Amber? Nope<br />
Sweet? Not really <br />
Versace Oud Noir and Prada Amber Pour Homme? Absolutely zero resemblance. <br />
<br />
Only thing in common with Prada APH is both are soapy but different types of soap.<br />
Prada is more like dove soap,  this smells similar to boraxo white powder soap. <br />
<br />
It's shaving cream with the smell of heath and woods with a creamy Tonka drydown. <br />
It's an astute Barbershop frag. Think barbershop in a royal palace.<br />
Best in its class IMO.<br />
<br />
Smell 10/10<br />
Performance 5/10<br />
<br />
Update: I've finally found something that resembles this ( I've been looking for about a year ) on the drydown.<br />
I bought B-612 and it smells like Lord George on the drydown. If you like B-612, you'll like this. However, I think Lord George slightly better if I had to choose just one.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1381156"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1381156#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1379837" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
