I get the shaving soap vibe much more than the rum, and I can sense a hint of tonka peering through. Definitely masculine, but I like wearing this as a woman as well. The first few minutes of the opening felt very strange and strong to me in a way I can't quite place, but it settles down quickly into a nice aftershave scent. It's not something that I personally want more of, especially at the price point for something that feels rather basic (albeit well-done), but I'll enjoy my sample! If you're into the old-fashioned men's shaving product sort of fragrances, give this one a try.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1379837"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1379837#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1375041" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Now I can save time, money and effort, and I can have this BO/after shave combo smell of debauchery in a second by spraying on The Tragedy of Lord George.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1353326"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1353326#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1349149" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1349149" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="redkettle"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1343348"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1343348.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="redkettle" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1349149ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1349149" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1343348">redkettle</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-05-25">05/25/21 12:44</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This review is based on a sample from the official 'Portraits Scent Library' sold by Penhaligons. <br />
<br />
Lord George opens ugly with several harsh notes (something oily, something soapy, something spicy, something animalic or leathery) which cannot be separated so it feels like a car crash. I find this very powerful and am surprised so many reviews say it is weak. It would give me a headache to wear it near my nose. I have the sample on my hand and that is too close. <br />
<br />
After a couple of hours, it dries down to something cold and metallic which reminds me of the surgical Chanel Égoïste Platinum (CEP) from the 1990s which smelt like an autopsy in a bottle. I disliked CEP so much that I gave the bottle away to Oxfam in the hope they could get some good out of reselling it. This Ice Age lasts at least four hours. Thus, combined with the confused and confusing opening, you get about six hours from a single spray. Not bad for a Penhaligons fragrance. <br />
<br />
To my nose, it seems Lord George on dry down is about 90% identical to CEP. The 10% difference is maybe a rose or geranium floweriness in George that tries to warm things up but fails - just like putting lipstick on an android cannot make it human. I get exactly zero booziness, tobacco smoke, vanilla/amber, tonka bean as reported by others or promised by the blurb. Maybe they are hidden behind the geranium, and trying to make it smell warm and fuzzy, and failing. <br />
<br />
I am bored by Lord George. If this sample is trustworthy, he has nothing original to offer. There are dozens of smellalikes out there, typically marketed at men, and have been for at least thirty years. All the same, if you do like this kind of fragrance - why not, it's a free world - I suggest comparing a sample of e.g. Chanel Égoïste Platinum and Penhaligons Lord George since you may be able to get the same effect, same quality, at a fraction of the cost. <br />
<br />
Although marketed at men, could a woman wear this? Why not? She would add something challenging, surprising, original to an otherwise passé, rather cynical rehash-product. I guess it depends on the woman (or man) wearing this to turn the generic into something more individual. Alternatively, if you fear to stand out, wearing this should be painless for most men, especially at work. But do not overspray as it is stronger than you might expect, especially at first. <br />
<br />
Verdict: Disappointing. Marketing hype over-promises. Generic product. Worth sampling but not worth buying a full bottle.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1349149"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1349149#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1334655" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1169218">Stephen N</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-03-24">03/24/19 23:19</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I once made fun of Penhaligon's on facebook (in a paid advertisement of theirs that came across my newsfeed no less) for being overpriced and very limited in their product offerings compared to Taylor of Old Bond Street.  After some back and forth with a few users, I relented and ordered a few samples of Penhaligon's fragrances, and of the ones I ordered... this was my favorite.<br />
<br />
I have gotten more compliments out of people over this fragrance than anything else I own.  Men, women, young and old, I have yet to meet anybody that does not like this fragrance.  I let a coworker of mine take a whiff of the sample, she got a bit of it on her hands, and she loved the smell of it so much she proceeded to rub her neck and hands down with it.  I thought she was going to clobber me for the rest of the vial.<br />
<br />
Needless to say, I don't make fun of Penhaligon's anymore.<br />
<br />
I may have to pick up a second job or figure out how to sell a kidney on the black market, but once I get the financing part figured out, there will be a bottle of this in my small collection of fragrances eventually.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1044437"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1044437#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1526907" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1526907" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="purplenoon"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1311284"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1311284.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="purplenoon" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Givenchy/Gentleman-Eau-de-Parfum-48476.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.48476.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Gentleman Eau de Parfum"title="Gentleman Eau de Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1526907ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1526907" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1311284">purplenoon</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-03-20">03/20/22 07:35</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I applied some of The Tragedy of Lord George from a sample before meeting friends for drinks at a cocktail bar, and it made me feel like a million dollars. Walking down the street I would catch whiffs of this that would make my heart skip, and rolling into the bar and taking off my scarf was one of the highlights of my week.<br />
<br />
This has a gorgeously sweet opening, warm and boozy but with a refreshing woodsy undertone and a faint pepper on top. As the pepper subsides, the amber comes out in full force, enveloping the wearer in a golden aura with a soapy undertone, a cross between Prada’s Amber Pour Homme and YSL’S Parfum Intense (incidentally, two of my favourite scents ever). The drydown is a spicy amber. All of this is masterfully blended; a stunning, stunning scent.<br />
<br />
While the scent itself is impeccable, the longevity is indeed a problem, as many have already noted. The fact that this barely lasts through a dinner party (at the end of which it is entirely a skin scent) is indeed the true Tragedy of Lord George. That said, I can’t bring myself to give it any less than a “love” in the ratings for this reason as the scent is just that good. It evokes old school sophistication and elegance while being entirely modern. Perfect for fall and winter, to enjoy with a nice scotch and in good company.<br />
<br />
EDIT: After another wear, I am indeed knocking Lord George down a peg to a "like" and not a "love" - a lesson learned for me not to be so enamoured by a fragrance on the first wear to the point where I entirely overlook its performance. While I do believe there is an ephemerality to fragrance that makes performance a matter of relative conditioning, I can't help but lament the fact that, on me, this turns into a skin scent in well under two hours. Maybe it's me and not Lord George; but in any case, it's gonna be a "like" for this sophisticated under-performer from me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1526907"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1526907#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1022851" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; What I get is a beautiful prominent shaving foam with a noticeable support of brandy and a hint of tonka. I get 0 amber. Not sure where that comes from.<br />
<br />
A great perfume, that said not worth full retail price. If looking for a barbershop fragrance, I'd suggest going for the beautiful Penhaligon's Sartorial, YSL Rive Gauche, Chanel Egoiste Platinum or MMM At The Barber's instead, which all retail for 3-4 times less, and are all great choices.<br />

Spring/Fall days, 30+</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1074213"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1074213#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1252415" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It's like a 19th century gentleman's club - with wood panelling, dim lighting, leather capitone sofas, heavy brandy glasses on the tables, the daily newspapers gently rustling in the smoke-filled air... I know there isn't any tobocco in the notes, but it may be the association that makes me distinctly smell it in the opening, along with heavy boozy notes. A few minutes in, there comes the scent of expensive soap (the type you'd find in a barber shop, to be used with high-quality shaving brushes made from goat hair). You can almost see the clean shaven skin of men in perfectly tailored suits sipping their first for the day. I don't love this fragrance, but it's very evocative for me - a whole scene in a bottle. And that considered I've never been in such a club.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="1252415"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=1252415#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="40716" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1029160">Melbourne man</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-05-15">05/15/17 16:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Tragedy of Lord George is one of Penhaligon’s Portrait Series released 2016.<br />
<br />
$268 AUD can get you a 75 ml bottle of this. That is one of the better prices I’ve seen quoted.<br />
<br />
Listed notes are brandy, amber (ambroxan), woody notes and tonka bean. Other sites also list shaving cream, which I do pick up.<br />
<br />
I was keen to smell this because of the brandy, but boy was it a fleeting whiff in the opening. Brandy for about 30 seconds and then straight into a heart of, well, shaving cream. Not even really classy smelling shaving cream of the Rive Gauche variety, but cheap shaving cream. I got no real wood notes and now in the dry down all I get is a sickly, plasticky ambroxan and tonka puddle.<br />
<br />
This was very disappointing from a house that I keep wanting to like, but apart from a couple of fragrances, has continued to disappoint.<br />
<br />
Don’t let the impressive looking bottle and cap fool you, I think it’s meant to be a distraction from how cheap this fragrance actually smells.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40716"comment_id="822992"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Penhaligon-s/The-Tragedy-of-Lord-George-40716.html?ccid=822992#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent865464" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1061765">cocolover56</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-09-28">09/28/17 07:30</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>In complete agreement with Melbourne Man here, sadly. Having received this as a sample from the same service. I wanted to love it for the same reason, but all I got was a screechy metallic mess. <br />
<br />
Yes, I may not get it and yes, I may have it in for Penhaligon's that overcharge quite criminally BUT I do know that this scent isn't nearly as complex as it sounds. <br />
<br />
Starts out somewhat interestingly, then it just devolves into an 'ambroxan and tonka puddle' with strong and harsh metallics going on in the back ground. <br />
